GT: c0*(-c1 + P/c2)*(c3 - P/c4)*P + c5*(c6 - P/c7)*P + c8*(c9 - exp(-c10*P))*P

I need to analyze the Ground Truth (GT) expression and determine if any candidate can match it.

**Step 1: Simplify the GT expression.**

The GT is:
```
0.17*(P/1.047 - 1)*(1 - P/10.21)*P + 0.17*(1 - P/10.21)*P + 0.17*(1 - exp(-0.097*P))*P
```

Let me expand each term:

**Term 1:** `0.17*(P/1.047 - 1)*(1 - P/10.21)*P`
= 0.17*(P/1.047 - 1)*(1 - P/10.21)*P

Expanding (P/1.047 - 1)*(1 - P/10.21):
= P/1.047 - P²/(1.047×10.21) - 1 + P/10.21
= -P²/10.69 + P(1/1.047 + 1/10.21) - 1

So Term 1 = 0.17*P*[-P²/10.69 + P×1.053 - 1]
= 0.17*(-P³/10.69 + 1.053P² - P)

**Term 2:** `0.17*(1 - P/10.21)*P`
= 0.17*(P - P²/10.21)

**Term 3:** `0.17*(1 - exp(-0.097*P))*P`
= 0.17*(P - P*exp(-0.097*P))

Combining all terms (polynomial parts):
- P³: -0.17/10.69 ≈ -0.0159
- P²: 0.17×1.053 - 0.17/10.21 ≈ 0.179 - 0.0166 ≈ 0.1624
- P: -0.17 + 0.17 + 0.17 = 0.17
- Non-polynomial: -0.17*P*exp(-0.097*P)

So GT ≈ -0.0159*P³ + 0.1624*P² + 0.17*P - 0.17*P*exp(-0.097*P)

**Step 2: The GT has the form: polynomial in P + P*exp(c*P) term, with NO dependence on t.**

Any candidate with t-dependence can only match if all t-dependent terms can be zeroed out.

**Step 3: Check candidates that are purely in P with an exponential term.**

Looking for: P³ + P² + P + P*exp(c*P) or similar structures.

**Candidate 3:** `P³(c0+c1) + P²(c2+c3+c4) + P*c5 + c7*P^c6*log(c8*P+1)`
The last term is P^c6 * log(c8*P+1). This can't become P*exp(aP).

**Candidate 14:** `P³*c0 + P²(c1+c2) + P*c3 + c4*t/(c5+t²) + c6*exp(P*c7)`
Setting c4=0: `P³*c0 + P²*c1' + P*c3 + c6*exp(c7*P)`. But we need P*exp(cP), not exp(cP). Close but not exact.

**Candidate 37:** `P³*c0 + P²(c1+c2) + P*c3 + c4*t*exp(c5*t) + c6*exp(P*c7 + c8*t)`
Setting c4=0, c8=0: `P³*c0 + P²*c1' + P*c3 + c6*exp(c7*P)`. Same issue - exp(cP) not P*exp(cP).

**Candidate 44:** `P³*c0 + P²*c1 + c3*P^c2*exp(c4*t) + c5*log(c6*exp(c7*P)+1)`
Setting c4=0, c2=1: `P³*c0 + P²*c1 + c3*P + c5*log(c6*exp(c7*P)+1)`. The log term isn't P*exp(cP).

**Candidate 46:** `P⁴c0/(P+c1) + P³(c2+c3)/(P+c1) + P²(c4+c5)/(P+c1) + P(c6+c7)/(P+c1) + c9*P^c8`
This is a rational function in P plus P^c8. This can't produce P*exp(cP).

None of the candidates can produce the P*exp(c*P) term present in the GT. The GT fundamentally contains a transcendental term P*exp(-0.097P) that none of the candidates can replicate exactly.

GT: c0*(-c1 + P/c2)*(c3 - P/c4)*P + c5*(c6 - P/c7)*P + c8*(c9 - exp(-c10*P))*P

I need to analyze the Ground Truth (GT) expression and compare it with each candidate.

## GT Analysis

The GT numerical expression is:
```
0.1699888096710614*(-1 + P/1.0472843670254641)*(1 - P/10.210545156320043)*P 
+ 0.1699888096710614*(1 - P/10.210545156320043)*P 
+ 0.1699888096710614*(1 - exp(-0.09709294493863778*P))*P
```

Let me simplify. Let me denote α = 0.16999, a = 1.04728, b = 10.2105, k = 0.09709.

**First term:** α*(-1 + P/a)*(1 - P/b)*P
= α*(P/a - 1)*(1 - P/b)*P

**Second term:** α*(1 - P/b)*P

**Third term:** α*(1 - exp(-k*P))*P

Let me combine the first two terms (both have factor α*(1 - P/b)*P):
α*(1 - P/b)*P * [(-1 + P/a) + 1] = α*(1 - P/b)*P * (P/a)
= α*P²/a * (1 - P/b)
= α*P²/a - α*P³/(a*b)

So the polynomial part from terms 1+2:
= α/a * P² - α/(a*b) * P³

The third term:
= α*P - α*P*exp(-k*P)

**Total GT:**
GT = -α/(a*b) * P³ + α/a * P² + α*P - α*P*exp(-k*P)

So GT = A*P³ + B*P² + C*P - C*P*exp(-k*P)

where:
- A = -α/(a*b) ≈ -0.16999/(1.04728*10.2105) ≈ -0.01589
- B = α/a ≈ 0.16999/1.04728 ≈ 0.16227
- C = α ≈ 0.16999
- k ≈ 0.09709

So GT = A*P³ + B*P² + C*P*(1 - exp(-k*P))

**Key observation:** The GT contains a term P*exp(-k*P), which is NOT a polynomial, rational, trigonometric, or logarithmic function. It's a specific exponential-times-polynomial form.

The GT is a function of P only (no t dependence).

Now let me check each candidate:

### Candidates with t-dependence that can't be zeroed:

**Candidate 1:** Has `c4*t*exp(c5*t)` - set c4=0. Becomes P³c0 + P²c1 + P(c2+c3) + c6. This is a cubic polynomial in P plus a constant. Missing the exp(-kP) term. **NO MATCH**
